COPALA Submissions and Applications
 Northside=92s COPALA (Celebration of Performing and Literary Arts) is now
accepting script submissions! COPALA is an annual performance of one or
multiple student-written, student-acted, student-directed, and
student-staged one-act plays.

If you would like to see your script brought to life, email it to Mr.
Nifong at wnifong@cps.edu by *Wednesday, April 3*. You may submit as many
as you like, but all submissions should be complete and refined.
 If you are interested in directing, email Mr. Nifong for more information
about the application process by *Tuesday, April 2,* at the latest.
 Auditions will occur in early April, and the performance will be in late
May.
Questions? Email Mr. Nifong at wnifong@cps.edu.

*Patientia virtutem sapientem facit.

Bienvenue Emilie de Rodat <http://rodat.fr/>!

NCP is delighted to welcome 10 students from Toulouse,
France<http://www.toulouse.fr/accueil>!
They will be staying with NCP families whose students take either French
III or IV; they are the equivalent of high school juniors. On Thursday 2/14
and Friday 2/22, the French students will shadow their NCP host-student.
They will be here from 2/13 =96 2/23. Please make them feel welcome during
their stay here in Chicago!
